  User=cc
  WorkingDirectory=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen
  ExecStart=/home/cc/micromamba/envs/cachelib-py-3.11/bin/jupyter lab --no-browser --ip=0.0.0.0 --NotebookApp.token='' --NotebookApp.password=''
  Restart=always
  RestartSec=10
  [Install]
  WantedBy=multi-user.target
  EOF`

  current progress
  The Dockerfile has been created with the basic structure including Ubuntu 22.04 base image, necessary system packages installation, repository cloning with submodules, directory structure creation, and gitignore files setup. However, the build failed at the micromamba installation step with exit code 109, indicating an issue with the tar extraction or micromamba initialization process.
  next step
  Fix the micromamba installation by creating the target directory first and adjusting the extraction command. Replace the failing RUN command with:
  ```dockerfile
  RUN mkdir -p /opt/bin && \
      curl -Ls https://micro.mamba.pm/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest | tar -xvj bin/micromamba -C /opt && \
      /opt/bin/micromamba shell init -s bash -p /opt/micromamba && \
      echo "micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11" >> ~/.bashrc
  ```

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH=/opt/micromamba/bin:$PATH
  ENV MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX=/opt/micromamba
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      curl \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      systemd \
      sudo \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git . && \
      if [ ! -d "BCacheSim" ]; then echo "Error: BCacheSim not found"; exit 1; fi && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN mkdir -p data runs tmp notebooks/figs notebooks/paper-figs/figs \
      data/tectonic/201910/Region1 \
      tmp/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/baleen/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/rejectx \
      runs/example/baleen/prefetch_ml-on-partial-hit
  RUN if [ ! -f data/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n!.gitignore\n!*.sh' > data/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN if [ ! -f runs/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n.ipynb_checkpoints\n!.gitignore\n!config.json\n!*/' > runs/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN curl -Ls https://micro.mamba.pm/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest | tar -xvj -C /opt && \
      /opt/bin/micromamba shell init -s bash -p /opt/micromamba && \
      echo "micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11" >> ~/.bashrc
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN source ~/.bashrc && \
      micromamba create -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 python=3.11 && \
      micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && \
      if [ -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml ]; then \
          micromamba env update -n cachelib-py-3.11 -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml; \
      elif [ -f BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt ]; then \
          pip install -r BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt; \
      fi && \
      micromamba install -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 -c conda-forge jupyterlab
  RUN chmod -R 755 /workspace
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  cd /workspace/data\n\
  if [ ! -f "tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace" ]; then\n\
      echo "Downloading trace files..."\n\
      if [ -f "get-tectonic.sh" ]; then\n\
          bash get-tectonic.sh\n\
      else\n\
          mkdir -p tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          cd tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          wget -q https://ftp.pdl.cmu.edu/pub/datasets/Baleen24/tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace\n\
      fi\n\
  fi\n\
  cd /workspace' > /workspace/download_traces.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/download_traces.sh
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  source /opt/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /workspace\n\

      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH=/opt/micromamba/bin:$PATH
  ENV MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX=/opt/micromamba
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      curl \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      systemd \
      sudo \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git . && \
      if [ ! -d "BCacheSim" ]; then echo "Error: BCacheSim not found"; exit 1; fi && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN mkdir -p data runs tmp notebooks/figs notebooks/paper-figs/figs \
      data/tectonic/201910/Region1 \
      tmp/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/baleen/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/rejectx \
      runs/example/baleen/prefetch_ml-on-partial-hit
  RUN if [ ! -f data/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n!.gitignore\n!*.sh' > data/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN if [ ! -f runs/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n.ipynb_checkpoints\n!.gitignore\n!config.json\n!*/' > runs/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN mkdir -p /opt/bin && \
      curl -Ls https://micro.mamba.pm/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest | tar -xvj bin/micromamba -C /opt && \
      /opt/bin/micromamba shell init -s bash -p /opt/micromamba && \
      echo "micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11" >> ~/.bashrc
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN source ~/.bashrc && \
      micromamba create -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 python=3.11 && \
      micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && \
      if [ -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml ]; then \
          micromamba env update -n cachelib-py-3.11 -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml; \
      elif [ -f BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt ]; then \
          pip install -r BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt; \
      fi && \
      micromamba install -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 -c conda-forge jupyterlab
  RUN chmod -R 755 /workspace
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  cd /workspace/data\n\
  if [ ! -f "tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace" ]; then\n\
      echo "Downloading trace files..."\n\
      if [ -f "get-tectonic.sh" ]; then\n\
          bash get-tectonic.sh\n\
      else\n\
          mkdir -p tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          cd tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          wget -q https://ftp.pdl.cmu.edu/pub/datasets/Baleen24/tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace\n\
      fi\n\
  fi\n\
  cd /workspace' > /workspace/download_traces.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/download_traces.sh
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  source /opt/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /workspace\n\
  exec "$@"' > /entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/entrypoint.sh"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      if [ ! -d "BCacheSim" ]; then echo "Error: BCacheSim not found"; exit 1; fi && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN mkdir -p data runs tmp notebooks/figs notebooks/paper-figs/figs \
      data/tectonic/201910/Region1 \
      tmp/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/baleen/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/rejectx \
      runs/example/baleen/prefetch_ml-on-partial-hit
  RUN if [ ! -f data/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n!.gitignore\n!*.sh' > data/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN if [ ! -f runs/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n.ipynb_checkpoints\n!.gitignore\n!config.json\n!*/' > runs/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN mkdir -p /opt/bin && \
      curl -Ls https://micro.mamba.pm/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest | tar -xvj -C /opt/bin && \
      chmod +x /opt/bin/micromamba && \
      /opt/bin/micromamba shell init -s bash -p /opt/micromamba && \
      echo "micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11" >> ~/.bashrc
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN source ~/.bashrc && \
      micromamba create -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 python=3.11 && \
      micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && \
      if [ -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml ]; then \
          micromamba env update -n cachelib-py-3.11 -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml; \
      elif [ -f BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt ]; then \
          pip install -r BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt; \
      fi && \
      micromamba install -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 -c conda-forge jupyterlab
  RUN chmod -R 755 /workspace
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  cd /workspace/data\n\
  if [ ! -f "tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace" ]; then\n\
      echo "Downloading trace files..."\n\
      if [ -f "get-tectonic.sh" ]; then\n\
          bash get-tectonic.sh\n\
      else\n\
          mkdir -p tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          cd tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          wget -q https://ftp.pdl.cmu.edu/pub/datasets/Baleen24/tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace\n\
      fi\n\
  fi\n\
  cd /workspace' > /workspace/download_traces.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/download_traces.sh
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  source /opt/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /workspace\n\
  exec "$@"' > /entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/entrypoint.sh"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 3 ---

  exec "$@"' > /entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/entrypoint.sh"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

          wget -q https://ftp.pdl.cmu.edu/pub/datasets/Baleen24/tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace\n\
      fi\n\
  fi\n\
  cd /workspace' > /workspace/download_traces.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/download_traces.sh
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  source /opt/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /workspace\n\
  exec "$@"' > /entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/entrypoint.sh"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH=/opt/micromamba/bin:$PATH
  ENV MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX=/opt/micromamba
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      curl \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      systemd \
      sudo \
      tar \
      bzip2 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git . && \
      if [ ! -d "BCacheSim" ]; then echo "Error: BCacheSim not found"; exit 1; fi && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN mkdir -p data runs tmp notebooks/figs notebooks/paper-figs/figs \
      data/tectonic/201910/Region1 \
      tmp/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/baleen/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/rejectx \
      runs/example/baleen/prefetch_ml-on-partial-hit
  RUN if [ ! -f data/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n!.gitignore\n!*.sh' > data/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN if [ ! -f runs/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n.ipynb_checkpoints\n!.gitignore\n!config.json\n!*/' > runs/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN mkdir -p /opt/micromamba/bin && \
      cd /opt/micromamba/bin && \
      curl -Ls https://micro.mamba.pm/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest | tar -xvj && \
      chmod +x /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba && \
      /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba shell init -s bash -p /opt/micromamba && \
      echo "micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11" >> ~/.bashrc
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN source ~/.bashrc && \
      micromamba create -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 python=3.11 && \
      micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && \
      if [ -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml ]; then \
          micromamba env update -n cachelib-py-3.11 -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml; \
      elif [ -f BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt ]; then \
          pip install -r BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt; \
      fi && \
      micromamba install -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 -c conda-forge jupyterlab
  RUN chmod -R 755 /workspace
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  cd /workspace/data\n\
  if [ ! -f "tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace" ]; then\n\
      echo "Downloading trace files..."\n\
      if [ -f "get-tectonic.sh" ]; then\n\
          bash get-tectonic.sh\n\
      else\n\
          mkdir -p tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          cd tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          wget -q https://ftp.pdl.cmu.edu/pub/datasets/Baleen24/tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace\n\
      fi\n\
  fi\n\
  cd /workspace' > /workspace/download_traces.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/download_traces.sh
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  source /opt/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /workspace\n\
  exec "$@"' > /entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/entrypoint.sh"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH=/opt/micromamba/bin:$PATH
  ENV MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX=/opt/micromamba
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      curl \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      systemd \
      sudo \
      tar \
      bzip2 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git . && \
      if [ ! -d "BCacheSim" ]; then echo "Error: BCacheSim not found"; exit 1; fi && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN mkdir -p data runs tmp notebooks/figs notebooks/paper-figs/figs \
      data/tectonic/201910/Region1 \
      tmp/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/baleen/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/rejectx \
      runs/example/baleen/prefetch_ml-on-partial-hit
  RUN if [ ! -f data/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n!.gitignore\n!*.sh' > data/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN if [ ! -f runs/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n.ipynb_checkpoints\n!.gitignore\n!config.json\n!*/' > runs/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN mkdir -p /opt/micromamba && \
      cd /opt/micromamba && \
      curl -Ls https://micro.mamba.pm/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest | tar -xvj bin/micromamba && \
      chmod +x /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba && \
      /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba shell init -s bash -p /opt/micromamba && \
      echo "micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11" >> ~/.bashrc
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN source ~/.bashrc && \
      micromamba create -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 python=3.11 && \
      micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && \
      if [ -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml ]; then \
          micromamba env update -n cachelib-py-3.11 -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml; \
      elif [ -f BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt ]; then \
          pip install -r BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt; \
      fi && \
      micromamba install -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 -c conda-forge jupyterlab
  RUN chmod -R 755 /workspace
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  cd /workspace/data\n\
  if [ ! -f "tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace" ]; then\n\
      echo "Downloading trace files..."\n\
      if [ -f "get-tectonic.sh" ]; then\n\
          bash get-tectonic.sh\n\
      else\n\
          mkdir -p tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          cd tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          wget -q https://ftp.pdl.cmu.edu/pub/datasets/Baleen24/tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace\n\
      fi\n\
  fi\n\
  cd /workspace' > /workspace/download_traces.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/download_traces.sh
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  source /opt/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /workspace\n\
  exec "$@"' > /entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/entrypoint.sh"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH=/opt/micromamba/bin:$PATH
  ENV MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX=/opt/micromamba
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      curl \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      systemd \
      sudo \
      tar \
      bzip2 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git . && \
      if [ ! -d "BCacheSim" ]; then echo "Error: BCacheSim not found"; exit 1; fi && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN mkdir -p data runs tmp notebooks/figs notebooks/paper-figs/figs \
      data/tectonic/201910/Region1 \
      tmp/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/baleen/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/rejectx \
      runs/example/baleen/prefetch_ml-on-partial-hit
  RUN if [ ! -f data/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n!.gitignore\n!*.sh' > data/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN if [ ! -f runs/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n.ipynb_checkpoints\n!.gitignore\n!config.json\n!*/' > runs/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN mkdir -p /opt/micromamba && \
      cd /tmp && \
      wget -q https://micro.mamba.pm/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest -O micromamba.tar.bz2 && \
      tar -xjf micromamba.tar.bz2 && \
      mv bin/micromamba /opt/micromamba/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba && \
      rm -rf /tmp/micromamba.tar.bz2 /tmp/bin && \
      /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba shell init -s bash -p /opt/micromamba && \
      echo "micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11" >> ~/.bashrc
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN source ~/.bashrc && \
      micromamba create -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 python=3.11 && \
      micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && \
      if [ -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml ]; then \
          micromamba env update -n cachelib-py-3.11 -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml; \
      elif [ -f BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt ]; then \
          pip install -r BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt; \
      fi && \
      micromamba install -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 -c conda-forge jupyterlab
  RUN chmod -R 755 /workspace
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  cd /workspace/data\n\
  if [ ! -f "tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace" ]; then\n\
      echo "Downloading trace files..."\n\
      if [ -f "get-tectonic.sh" ]; then\n\
          bash get-tectonic.sh\n\
      else\n\
          mkdir -p tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          cd tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          wget -q https://ftp.pdl.cmu.edu/pub/datasets/Baleen24/tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace\n\
      fi\n\
  fi\n\
  cd /workspace' > /workspace/download_traces.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/download_traces.sh
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  source /opt/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /workspace\n\
  exec "$@"' > /entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/entrypoint.sh"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH=/opt/micromamba/bin:$PATH
  ENV MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX=/opt/micromamba
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      curl \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      systemd \
      sudo \
      tar \
      bzip2 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git . && \
      if [ ! -d "BCacheSim" ]; then echo "Error: BCacheSim not found"; exit 1; fi && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN mkdir -p data runs tmp notebooks/figs notebooks/paper-figs/figs \
      data/tectonic/201910/Region1 \
      tmp/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/baleen/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/rejectx \
      runs/example/baleen/prefetch_ml-on-partial-hit
  RUN if [ ! -f data/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n!.gitignore\n!*.sh' > data/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN if [ ! -f runs/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n.ipynb_checkpoints\n!.gitignore\n!config.json\n!*/' > runs/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN mkdir -p /opt/micromamba/bin
  RUN cd /tmp && \
      wget -q https://micro.mamba.pm/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest -O micromamba.tar.bz2 && \
      tar -xjf micromamba.tar.bz2 && \
      if [ -f bin/micromamba ]; then \
          mv bin/micromamba /opt/micromamba/bin/; \
      else \
          echo "Error: micromamba binary not found after extraction"; \
          exit 1; \
      fi && \
      chmod +x /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba && \
      rm -rf /tmp/micromamba.tar.bz2 /tmp/bin
  RUN /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba shell init -s bash -p /opt/micromamba && \
      echo "micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11" >> ~/.bashrc
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN source ~/.bashrc && \
      micromamba create -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 python=3.11 && \
      micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && \
      if [ -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml ]; then \
          micromamba env update -n cachelib-py-3.11 -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml; \
      elif [ -f BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt ]; then \
          pip install -r BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt; \
      fi && \
      micromamba install -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 -c conda-forge jupyterlab
  RUN chmod -R 755 /workspace
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  cd /workspace/data\n\
  if [ ! -f "tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace" ]; then\n\
      echo "Downloading trace files..."\n\
      if [ -f "get-tectonic.sh" ]; then\n\
          bash get-tectonic.sh\n\
      else\n\
          mkdir -p tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          cd tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          wget -q https://ftp.pdl.cmu.edu/pub/datasets/Baleen24/tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace\n\
      fi\n\
  fi\n\
  cd /workspace' > /workspace/download_traces.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/download_traces.sh
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  source /opt/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /workspace\n\
  exec "$@"' > /entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/entrypoint.sh"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH=/opt/micromamba/bin:$PATH
  ENV MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX=/opt/micromamba
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      curl \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      systemd \
      sudo \
      tar \
      bzip2 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git . && \
      if [ ! -d "BCacheSim" ]; then echo "Error: BCacheSim not found"; exit 1; fi && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN mkdir -p data runs tmp notebooks/figs notebooks/paper-figs/figs \
      data/tectonic/201910/Region1 \
      tmp/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/baleen/example/201910_Region1_0_0.1 \
      runs/example/rejectx \
      runs/example/baleen/prefetch_ml-on-partial-hit
  RUN if [ ! -f data/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n!.gitignore\n!*.sh' > data/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN if [ ! -f runs/.gitignore ]; then \
      echo -e '*\n.ipynb_checkpoints\n!.gitignore\n!config.json\n!*/' > runs/.gitignore; \
      fi
  RUN mkdir -p /opt/micromamba/bin
  RUN cd /tmp && \
      wget -q https://micro.mamba.pm/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest -O micromamba.tar.bz2 && \
      tar -xjf micromamba.tar.bz2 && \
      if [ -f bin/micromamba ]; then \
          mv bin/micromamba /opt/micromamba/bin/; \
      else \
          echo "Error: micromamba binary not found after extraction"; \
          exit 1; \
      fi && \
      chmod +x /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba && \
      rm -rf /tmp/micromamba.tar.bz2 /tmp/bin
  RUN /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba create -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 python=3.11 --root-prefix /opt/micromamba
  RUN if [ -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml ]; then \
          /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba env update -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml --root-prefix /opt/micromamba; \
      elif [ -f BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt ]; then \
          /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba run -n cachelib-py-3.11 --root-prefix /opt/micromamba pip install -r BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt; \
      fi
  RUN /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba install -y -n cachelib-py-3.11 -c conda-forge jupyterlab --root-prefix /opt/micromamba
  RUN chmod -R 755 /workspace
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  cd /workspace/data\n\
  if [ ! -f "tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace" ]; then\n\
      echo "Downloading trace files..."\n\
      if [ -f "get-tectonic.sh" ]; then\n\
          bash get-tectonic.sh\n\
      else\n\
          mkdir -p tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          cd tectonic/201910/Region1\n\
          wget -q https://ftp.pdl.cmu.edu/pub/datasets/Baleen24/tectonic/201910/Region1/full_0_0.1.trace\n\
      fi\n\
  fi\n\
  cd /workspace' > /workspace/download_traces.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/download_traces.sh
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  export MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX=/opt/micromamba\n\
  export PATH=/opt/micromamba/bin:$PATH\n\
  cd /workspace\n\
  exec /opt/micromamba/bin/micromamba run -n cachelib-py-3.11 --root-prefix /opt/micromamba /bin/bash' > /entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/entrypoint.sh"]
